Mopatis_1 = {
	name = Illyrio # Canon, THE Illyrio Mopatis
	dynasty = dynn_Mopatis
	dna = Mopatis_1

	martial = 3
	diplomacy = 6
	intrigue = 10
	stewardship = 6
	learning = 3
	prowess = 5

	religion = rhllor_fc
	culture = pentoshi

	trait = education_stewardship_4
	trait = physique_good_1
	trait = greedy
	trait = ambitious
	trait = gregarious
	trait = charming

	disallow_random_traits = yes

	8255.1.1 = {
		birth = yes
		add_character_flag = has_scripted_appearance
		add_character_flag = canon_status_canon
	}
	8271.1.1 = {
		effect = { add_trait = education_martial_prowess_2 }
		effect = {
			change_current_weight = 20
			target_weight_modifier_effect = { VALUE = 20 }
			
		}
		add_character_flag = citadel_is_mopatis
	}
	8275.1.1 = { add_spouse = Narratys_57 } # Nerria Narratys, cousin to Prince of Pentos
	8279.1.1 = {
		effect = { remove_trait = education_martial_prowess_2 }
		trait = education_republican_knowledge_4
		trait = gluttonous
		trait = fashionable
		effect = {
			change_current_weight = 40
			target_weight_modifier_effect = { VALUE = 60 }
		}
	}
	8281.1.1 = {
		add_spouse = Mopatis_hh_1 # Serra
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { character:Narratys_1 = { is_alive = yes } }
				reverse_add_opinion = {
					target = character:Narratys_1 # Yoro Narratys
					modifier = insulted_opinion
				}
			}
			change_current_weight = 20
			target_weight_modifier_effect = { VALUE = 80 }
		}
	}
	8290.1.1 = {
		change_current_weight = 40
		target_weight_modifier_effect = { VALUE = 120 }
	}
}
### Household

		}
	}

	8284.1.1 = {
		trait = greyscale

	}
